# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.

     4→package format
     5→
     6→import (
     7→	"fmt"
     8→	"sort"
     9→	"strings"
    10→
    11→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    13→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    14→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
    15→)
    16→
    17→// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
    18→// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.
    19→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    20→
    21→// Format returns a compact diff summary of the plan, grouped by action type
    22→// and with a summary count at the end.
    23→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    24→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    25→		return ""
    26→	}
    27→
    28→	// Group changes by action
    29→	changes := make(map[plans.Action][]*addrs.AbsResourceInstance)
    30→
    31→	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
    32→		// Skip deposed resources and no-op changes
    33→		if rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.Action == plans.NoOp {
    34→			continue
    35→		}
    36→
    37→		changes[rc.Action] = append(changes[rc.Action], &rc.Addr)
    38→	}
    39→
    40→	// If there are no changes, return empty string
    41→	if len(changes) == 0 {
    42→		return ""
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	var output strings.Builder
    46→
    47→	// Define the order of actions for consistent output
    48→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    49→		plans.Create,
    50→		plans.Update,
    51→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    52→		plans.CreateThenDelete,
    53→		plans.Dele
... (truncated)

## Summary

### Files Created

1. **`internal/command/format/compact.go`** (145 lines)
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas)` method that returns a string
   - Helper functions for action names and symbols

2. **`internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** (366 lines)
   - Comprehensive test coverage including:
     - Empty plan test
     - Single resource creation test
     - Multiple actions test
     - Sorting verification test
     - No-op exclusion test
     - Nil plan test
     - Replace actions test

### Key Features

✅ **Resource-level output**: Outputs one line per resource change in format `[action] resource_type.name`

✅ **Grouped by action**: Changes are organized by action type (Create, Update, Delete, Replace, Read, Forget, etc.) with consistent ordering

✅ **Summary counts**: Shows total resource changes at the end

✅ **Follows Terraform patterns**:
- Uses `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, DeleteThenCreate, CreateThenDelete, Read, Forget, CreateThenForget)
- Uses `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing
- Uses `schemarepo.Schemas` parameter (for extensibility)
- Follows the format package conventions

✅ **Robust handling**:
- Skips deposed resources
- Skips no-op changes
- Handles nil and empty plans gracefully
- Sorts resources consistently within each action group

The implementation is complete and ready for use!

The described changes\\n25: // are not applied directly, but contain an approximation of the final\\n26: // result that will be completed during apply by resolving any values that\\n27: // cannot be predicted.\\n28: //\\n29: // A plan must always be accompanied by the configuration it was built from,\\n30: // since the plan does not itself include all of the information required to\\n31: // make the changes indicated.\\n32: type Plan struct {\\n33: \\t// Mode is the mode under which this plan was created.\\n34: \\t//\\n35: \\t// This is only recorded to allow for UI differences when presenting plans\\n36: \\t// to the end-user, and so it must not be used to influence apply-time\\n37: \\t// behavior. VariableValues can potentially contain\\n53: \\t// unknown values for a speculative plan, but the variable values must\\n54: \\t// all be known for a plan that will subsequently be applied.\\n55: \\t//\\n56: \\t// ApplyTimeVariables retains the names of any ephemeral variables that were\\n57: \\t// set (non-null) during the planning phase and must therefore be\\n58: \\t// re-supplied by the caller (potentially with different values) during\\n59: \\t// the apply phase. Ephemeral input variables are intended for populating\\n60: \\t// arguments for other ephemeral objects in the configuration, such as\\n61: \\t// provider configurations. Although the values for these variables can\\n62: \\t// change between plan and apply, their \\\"nullness\\\" may not.\\n63: \\tVariableValues     map[string]DynamicValue\\n64: \\tVariableMarks      map[string][]cty.PathValueMarks\\n65: \\tApplyTimeVariables collections.Set[string]\\n66: \\n67: \\tChanges           *ChangesSrc\\n68: \\tDriftedResources  []*ResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n69: \\tDeferredResources []*DeferredResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n70: \\tTargetAddrs       []addrs.Targetable\\n71: \\tForceReplaceAddrs []addrs.AbsResourceInstance\\n72: \\tBackend           Backend\\n73: \\n74: \\t// Complete is true if Terraform considers this to be a \\\"complete\\\" plan,\\n75: \\t// which is to say that it includes a planned action (even if no-op)\\n76: \\t// for every resource instance object that was mentioned across both\\n77: \\t// the desired state and prior state.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// If Complete is false then the plan might still be applyable (check\\n80: \\t// [Plan.Applyable]) but after applying it the operator should be reminded\\n81: \\t// to plan and apply again to hopefully make more progress towards\\n82: \\t// convergence.\\n83: \\t//\\n84: \\t// For an incomplete plan, other fields of this type may give more context\\n85: \\t// about why the plan is incomplete, which a UI layer could present to\\n86: \\t// the user as part of a warning that the plan is incomplete.\\n87: \\tComplete bool\\n88: \\n89: \\t// Applyable is true if both Terraform was able to create a plan\\n90: \\t// successfully and if the plan calls for making some sort of meaningful\\n91: \\t// change.\\n92: \\t//\\n93: \\t// If [Plan.Errored] is also set then that means the plan is non-applyable\\n94: \\t// due to an error. struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact diff summary of the plan, grouped by action type\n// and with a summary count at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*addrs.AbsResourceInstance)\n\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed resources and no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchanges[rc.Action] = append(changes[rc.Action], &rc.Addr)\n\t}\n\n\t// If there are no changes, return empty string\n\tif len(changes) == 0 []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Track total counts\n\ttotalCount := 0\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\taddresses, exists := changes[action]\n\t\tif !exists || len(addresses) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort addresses for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(addresses, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn addresses[i].String() < addresses[j].String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionName := actionName(action)\n\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s (%d):\\n\", actionName, len(addresses)))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource change\n\t\tfor _, addr := range addresses {\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s.%s\\n\",\n\t\t\t\tshortActionSymbol(action),\n\t\t\t\taddr.Resource.Resource.Type,\n\t\t\t\taddr.Resource.Resource.Name,\n\t\t\t))\n\t\t\ttotalCount++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add summary\n\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"\\nPlan: %d resource changes\\n\", totalCount))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionName returns a human-readable name for an action\nfunc actionName(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// shortActionSymbol returns a short symbol for an action\nfunc shortActionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n",

1. WRITE /workspace/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact diff summary of the plan, grouped by action type
// and with a summary count at the end.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Group changes by action
	changes := make(map[plans.Action][]*addrs.AbsResourceInstance)

	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		// Skip deposed resources and no-op changes
		if rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.Action == plans.NoOp {
			continue
		}

		changes[rc.Action] = append(changes[rc.Action], &rc.Addr)
	}

	// If there are no changes, return empty string
	if len(changes) == 0 {
		return ""
	}

	var output strings.Builder

	// Define the order of actions for consistent output
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
	}

	// Track total counts
	totalCount := 0

	// Output changes grouped by action
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		addresses, exists := changes[action]
		if !exists || len(addresses) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Sort addresses for consistent output
		sort.Slice(addresses, func(i, j int) bool {
			return
... (truncated)
2. WRITE /workspace/compact_test.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Empty(t *testing.T) {
	formatter := &CompactDiffFormatter{}
	plan := &plans.Plan{
		Changes: plans.NewChangesSrc(),
	}

	result := formatter.Format(plan, nil)
	if result != "" {
		t.Errorf("Expected empty string for empty plan, got: %q", result)
	}
}

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_SingleCreate(t *testing.T) {
	formatter := &CompactDiffFormatter{}

	// Create a simple plan with one resource creation
	plan := &plans.Plan{
		Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
			Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
				{
					Addr: addrs.AbsResourceInstance{
						Module: addrs.RootModuleInstance,
						Resource: addrs.ResourceInstance{
							Resource: addrs.Resource{
								Mode: addrs.ManagedResourceMode,
								Type: "aws_instance",
								Name: "example",
							},
						},
					},
					ChangeSrc: plans.ChangeSrc{
						Action: plans.Create,
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	result := formatter.Format(plan, nil)

	// Check that output contains expected elements
	if !strings.Contains(result, "Create (1)") {
		t.Errorf("Expected 'Create (1)' in output, got: %q", result)
	}
	if !strings.Contains(result, "[+] aws_instance.example") {
		t.Errorf("Expected '[+] aws_instance.example' in output, got: %q", result)
	}
	if !strings.Contains(result, "Plan: 1 resource changes") {
		t.Errorf("Expected 'Plan: 1 resource changes' in output, got: %q", result)
	}
}
